If you ever find yourself nostalgic for those days of your youth just a spray of Percival and you're right back there, hanging out with your friends, trying to look cool while pretending not to notice the shirtless models. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2305456" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Iron Chicken"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2041668"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Iron Chicken" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2305456ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2305456" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2041668">Iron Chicken</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-05">10/05/24 02:37</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This like all PDM is overpriced, however I have purchased twice and on both occasions gone through the bottle in around three Months, it's a fabulous fragrance and ticks many boxes but of course you can say it's generic / boring whatever and you can buy similar scents for much less. I have received more compliments wearing this than anything else, even when I never expected it. it does last 5-7 hours on my skin, maybe 5-6 sprays in the morning.<br />
<br />
I have re applied this after work as the scent is just so nice. I was always a creed fan and since their issues with performance I decided to give PDM Percival a try. I think I would purchase a third bottle once I have the available money.<br />
<br />
Percival has a fresh, lavender citrus opening which then fades after about an hour or so to the base notes, which are listed and correct. I am a fan of clean citrusy type fragrances, so this is a winner for me as it lasts unlike other similar style scents. If you have the cash and enjoy this type of fragrance it's worth buying, otherwise don't waste you money and purchase something cheaper. Although very expensive and in many ways overpriced, I would say the quality f the ingredients and the smell of this kind of makes up for the price tag. Recommended 9/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="2305456"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=2305456#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2304396" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It might smell generic, but people who say they dislike it probably haven’t given it a full wearing. I’ve had this for about half a year now, and I too had doubts about it in the first few months of owning it. It’s currently my favorite fresh fragrance next to l’immensite from LV. Performance is really strong, and this is one of the only scents that I consistently get compliments on (never from people I don’t know though). <br />
<br />
I would recommend getting a sample and wearing it for a full day. That way you’ll understand and appreciate a scent much more than just wearing one spray on your arm. Do I recommend it for the price? If you are already someone who has spent a lot of money on perfumes and only want the best, then yes. If you currently own and use a lot of designers and aren’t used to spending a lot of money on fragrances, then you might be disappointed at first. It's the difference between "mall smell" and a proper, nuanced fragrance. It's great.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="2282480"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=2282480#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2281915" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Here's my thoughts. <br />
1. Percival lasts much longer. I sprayed Percival on the back of my left hand, Legend Blue on my right hand. The next day I picked up a fruity amber smell when my hand was near my face and I thought "what's that" before I realized it was the Percival I sprayed the previous day on my left hand.<br />
2. Both are quite similar in the smell, but Percival smells much more Ambery, fruity, and woody. Much more Orange citrus in Percival. Legend Blue is a simpler smell, but it's not simple by any means.<br />
3. Price is hard to justify when Legend Blue exists. I already had a big bottle of Percival. But, if you're going for this kind of scent and you have $200 to spare, do this. Spend $50 on Legend Blue and spend the $150 on getting one or two other fragrances. Sad but true.<br />

Better to spray lightly for maximum effect.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="2254883"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=2254883#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2254561" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I know it's a designer profile but it's just obvious that this is extremely well blended and even though it has a lot of synthetics, I think people forget that there are synthetics that are more costly than others and synthetic doesn't automatically mean that it smells bad. The citruses in the opening are certainly VERY natural smelling to my nose. I find this very aromatic, and extremely crisp. I heard someone use the term 'ice flowers' and that represents this fragrance well. Call me crazy, but this is a white fragrance to me (not blue) - it almost smells translucent and clear. I get 10-12 hours of longevity with reform batch, and it's strong as piss. I sprayed four times to work last summer and I choked out my colleague that I sit directly next to. I have never received a compliment on this fragrance ever so I don't know if people love it, but it is extremely fresh so I doubt anyone strongly dislikes it. I think the compliment factor (or lack thereof) might also be that it is completely absent of sweetness (and I have received my fair share of compliments on other fragrances so this nothing to do with my appearance/vibe).</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2232703" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Maxmiller614"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2192051"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2192051.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Maxmiller614" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2232703ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2232703" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2192051">Maxmiller614</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-29">07/29/24 09:16</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Percival is where it's at. This is genuinely so good, but that price is a mood killer.<br />
<br />
This is like the more sophisticated, big brother to Abercrombie Fierce and Montblanc Legend, of which both are admittedly among my all-time favorites. It's citrusy, ambery, fresh, and has that fresh out of the shower feel. You'll feel clean and on point wearing this.<br />
<br />
I think Percival is truly modern perfumery for the modern man, but isn't bound to younger or older demographics. I think anyone can wear this and will be able to pull it off. <br />
<br />
The longevity is about 8 hours but I found it to be a little under that most times, sitting at about 6. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1846450">truthtea</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-10">07/10/24 12:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The highest quality niche version of the designer Fierce/Legend DNA with good ingredients. Smells just like the DNA but with better ingredients and blend, very fresh and blue so of course it smells mass-appealing designer. I got a headache with it and even nose-blind, but when sprayed anywhere but the front neck, you can still smell hints of this in the air hours later. If you can smell it in the air, people around can smell it too. <br />
<br />
Performance is pretty good lasting around 7-9 hours with a medium-loud projection with varying sprays (5-8) at least on my 2023 batch. Good price on discounters and perfect for the warmer weather and even the gym or as a signature scent.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="2214300"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=2214300#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2213205" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1043744">FreshLiving</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-06-20">06/20/24 14:18</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is the brother of Green Irish Tweed. Except this is blue, woody, mature as opposed to green, woody, mature.<br />
Once you smell it and see it, you will undoubtedly agree. I love it. <br />
<br />
I’ll be reaching for this at the start of spring, in summer days/nights, and earlier fall days before the leaves all fall and times transition in to the heavier fragrances. This is a fragrance that reminds you why you love fragrances so much.<br />
<br />
It may not be PdM’s greatest niche creation and release, or as imaginative as some of their heavier fall/winter fragrances, but this is a great offering and one that I’m sure will be a wardrobe staple. The more you spray and wear it, the more sense it makes; very dependable and one for many years I think. <br />
<br />
Who cares if it smells like others. Everything smells like something, no? But for the quality and ingredients here this works magic. Sure you can go with Mont Blanc or Dylan Blue instead since it’s nothing new like many draw on here. However those smell cheap, don’t last, give you nausea, this does not.<br />
<br />
Performance wise I’m not too impressed. Off of my bottle it projects for about 1.5 hours and then goes to a skin scent for the next 4-5 hours.<br />
Unless there’s something in here making me nose blind, this isn’t PdM’s best performer.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="2194481"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=2194481#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2186564" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; So it was nowhere near overpriced for me at the time.<br />
<br />
For the perfume itself, I do like the scent it gave off, which is soapy and out of the shower kind of vibe, <br />
but done right and done luxuriously. It performs great and has good longevity on my skin as well.<br />
<br />
The only issue I had with Percival is that, it just doesn't scream "niche" to me.<br />
It gave off a classy and dandy vibe, but not in a showy/showoff kind of way.<br />
I like it, but I want to look for a special occasion type of perfume for now.<br />
One that makes me excited to wear it on a date night type of vibe.<br />
Overall, it's a great perfume but TOO versatile for my needs.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="2178528"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=2178528#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2178039" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2060445">PK_thundr</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-17">04/17/24 22:54</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>A wonderful fresh fragrance. On my skin, it's fresh, woody, aromatic, amber, musky and lavender. The florals come through in a very masculine way. <br />
The opening (5-10 mins) does bring similarities to Montblanc Legend and Fierce, but this has a much better opening smell. To my nose it smells totally different after the opening. The mid and dry down smell completely different for Fierce and Legend, as in they are way worse. Legend EDP has this cheap ozonic suede smell Legend EDT dries down to a generic Tonka. <br />
The mid and the dry down bring these wonderful woody mahogany, amberwood, musk, florals, and hints of the fir. You can actually find all of these listed notes in the mid and drydown. It's wonderful and lasts for a long time. <br />
It's so good. This works for anything. <br />
I'm happy this has haters that gatekeep this scent for me nose. My nose tells me it's one of the best freshies.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="2128029"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=2128029#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2127626" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2127626" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="RGH01"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1331188"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1331188.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="RGH01" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2127626ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2127626" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1331188">RGH01</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-17">04/17/24 12:46</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Percival is a basic cheapie fragrance trying it’s hardest to be something luxurious, a sheep in wolfs clothing you might say. This plainly smells like overly-synthetic shower gel which is a scent profile that’s been played out to death on the designer market.<br />
<br />
Of course it smells pleasant, but the obscene amounts of ambroxan and amberwood make it smell the same as 90% of everything else on the market which you can get for a tenth of the price. I suppose there’s some hints of lavender and citrus but it is simply an ambroxan explosion unfortunately.<br />
<br />
Sorry to anyone that loves this but who is paying such ridiculous prices to smell like something that costs £10? I don’t understand it, got to be one of the worst releases from an already poor house.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="2127626"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=2127626#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2127263" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2123074" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Psalzarulo"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1723203"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="Psalzarulo" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2123074ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2123074" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1723203">Psalzarulo</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-12">04/12/24 19:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>On first impression, this is a super fresh, clean scent... it almost reminds me of a masculine shower or even a slightly grown-up Axe Body Spray. The top note is a blend of fresh citrus and green florals, along with clean lavender. I would also say this is similar to some designer "Blue" scents based on bright citrus and woody base, although this one adds some spice to the blend. <br />
<br />
I would say the scent profile is a mix of Bleu de Chanel and YSL La Suit de l'Homme; mainly because it mixes classic fresh blue notes with classic spicy/ boozy notes. <br />
<br />
I would say that, compared to the handful of other PdM scents I've tested, this is probably the most mainstream and least distinctive once I've smelled, although that's certainly not a bad thing. <br />
<br />
Overall, I would say this is a pretty disappointing offering from PdM. This is obviously a high quality scent with great performance, but I'm not really sure how it's really worth two or three times as much as a similar-smelling designer scent. Keeping the significantly high price in mind, I give this a 7.75/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="2123074"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=2123074#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2120402" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Performs really well too</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="2118810"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=2118810#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2118808" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.79);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2118808" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="MrBolton"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1161847"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1161847.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="MrBolton" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Creed/Himalaya-465.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.465.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Himalaya"title="Himalaya"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2118808ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2118808" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1161847">MrBolton</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-08">04/08/24 20:59</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>After much debate, I decided that I needed this in the collection. Opted for the 2.5 oz bottle because you can’t fly with the 4.2 oz. Weird sizing.<br />
This is the generic men’s blue fragrance done exceptionally well. It is a classically modern masculine scent and is fresh, but still a bit heavy. I don’t think I’d want to wear this outside in super high heat. It’s a bit too “aromatic” for that when there are better fresh citrus options out there, although this wouldn’t be a terrible option. Definitely a signature scent worthy choice and easy to wear to about any occasion on any day. It’s what us enthusiasts would call a “dumb reach” because you don’t have to think about it. It just works. <br />
<br />
How close is it to Mont Blanc Legend? Very. I’ve only compared it to Legend EDT, but it is remarkably similar in all but performance. I can get a full work day out of this with still having some projection. Percival also smells higher quality and more natural in its ingredients versus its more synthetic competitor Legend. If on a budget, Legend is a no-brainer where you can get a huge size for less than half the price of the smaller Percival. However, you’re going to use double the sprays to come anywhere close to Percival’s performance. Not sure on MB Legend EDP if that’s not an issue. <br />
<br />
Versus Vodka on the Rocks By Kilian, it doesn’t feel too redundant owning both, unless you want to have a smaller collection. VOTR is the fresher cousin. Performance isn’t as good on VOTR. I like them evenly, but I guess would choose Percival if I only could keep one. Just is more versatile.<br />
<br />
I plan to keep a bottle in my collection always going forward. It is blind buy safe if you like what you’ve read.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="2118808"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=2118808#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2118003" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The scent is actually pretty darn good. It's got this nice blend of smells that just work well together, you know? It's not overpowering or anything, just a solid, pleasant aroma.<br />
<br />
One thing I can say about it is that it's super versatile. You could wear it to pretty much any occasion, whether you're heading out for a fancy dinner or just chilling with friends. It's the kind of scent that fits in no matter what time of day it is. Plus, people are definitely going to tell you that you smell good when you're wearing it.<br />
<br />
But here's the thing—it's not exactly memorable. Like, yeah, it smells good, but it's not the kind of scent that's going to stick with you. It's kind of forgettable, you know? You wear it, people say you smell nice, and then it's like, "Eh, what was that scent again?"<br />
<br />
And get this—it's supposed to be a niche fragrance, but honestly, it feels more like something you'd find at your average department store. I mean, don't get me wrong, it's a decent fragrance, but it's not exactly worth the higher price tag.<br />
<br />
So yeah, overall, it's a good fragrance for sure. But if you're looking for something that really stands out and leaves a lasting impression, this might not be it. Would probably not buy again, but if you can get a great deal on it, I think it might be more worth the money.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="2082186"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=2082186#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2076754" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I quite like it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="2076389"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=2076389#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2070230" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2070230" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="zhejr"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/968637"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="zhejr" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2070230ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x0"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2070230" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.8); align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="2070230"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=2070230#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2069662" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2069662" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="TheDogfatherHTX"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1824841"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1824841.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="TheDogfatherHTX" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Carolina-Herrera/Bad-Boy-Extreme-78562.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.78562.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Bad Boy Extreme"title="Bad Boy Extreme"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2069662ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2069662" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1824841">TheDogfatherHTX</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-02-21">02/21/24 12:43</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is a Parfums De Marly scent that has received a fair amount of hype within the fragrance community. Not as much hype as Layton, mind you; but still a fair amount. I got a sample of this from the SB subscription box so I could give it a proper review. Here's how it went;<br />
<br />
Scent:<br />
Opening is citrusy, floral, and woody. The primary notes I get are ambroxan, lavender, orange, and geranium. The strongest of the notes are the orange and lavender. The orange provides a juicy citrus accord while the lavender brings a soft, floral, aromatic quality. This is followed by a masculine ambery woodiness from the ambroxan accompanied by a rosy, floral note from the geranium. I also get hints of the bergamot, jasmine, hedione, balsam fir, and clearwood; but they play more of a supporting role to the other more prominent notes. The dry down is ambery, woody, and floral. The primary notes I get are ambroxan, lavender, amberwood, and violet. The strongest of the notes are the ambroxan and lavender. The ambroxan is still bringing that same big dose of ambery woodiness from the opening along with the soft floral touches of the lavender. Following closely is the amberwood for more ambery woods paired with powdery florals from the violet. The balsam fir and clearwood are still there as well helping to boost the woodiness of the scent.<br />
<br />
Performance:<br />
Initial projection is strong at around 6 feet. Sillage matches that with an easily noticeable scent trail. After about 4 hours the projection was still further than arms length and the scent trail was still easily noticeable. At the 8 hour mark the projection and scent trail were unchanged. I went to bed and after waking up the projection was gone but there was still a faint scent trail; this was about 16 hours after I sprayed it on. Certified beast mode performance.<br />
<br />
When to wear:<br />
I feel this is a fragrance that would work in any weather, hot or cold, and for any occasion. Gentle enough for office wear, but alluring enough for a date night too.<br />
<br />
Blind buy:<br />
I don't really have anything else in my collection that I can adequately compare it to; but if you like woody and floral scents that are still masculine this is a safe blind buy for you. <br />
<br />
Final Verdict:<br />
This is my first review of a Parfums De Marly fragrance. I went into this knowing that PDM fragrances have a reputation for being top tier, but I was somehow still surprised at the sheer performance of this fragrance. Not only that, but it was evident from the beginning that this fragrance was made with high quality ingredients, nicer than that of your typical designer fragrances. Overall, I would say this was a terrific first impression with the house. The scent itself may not be one of my favorites, but I can absolutely appreciate the craftsmanship and the power this fragrance puts out. I will definitely be trying more PDM's in the future.<br />
<br />
Scent: 7/10<br />
Longevity: 10/10<br />
Sillage: 9/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="2069662"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=2069662#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2068400" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2011425" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="kgkuntryluvr"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1942706"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="kgkuntryluvr" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2011425ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2011425" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1942706">kgkuntryluvr</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-12-26">12/26/23 15:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I finally decided to sample Percival side-by-side with my old bottle of Legend to see if it was worth upgrading when my bottle of Legend empties. To me, they are very similar but not nearly close enough to say that Percival is an exact dupe- I don't recall Fierce enough to say how close it is to that. While they aren't wildly different, Percival just does everything that Legend does better. It projects and lasts much more, while also having its own nuances that make it a little more interesting (though neither wow me). To make sure I wasn't being biased, I had my wife and daughters blind smell them and got 3 different opinions. My wife absolutely LOVED Percival. She couldn't tell me why she preferred it over the other hand, but she said there was just "something special" about it. My youngest daughter chose Legend because she thought Percival was too strong and "cologney". My teenage daughter chose Percival for the exact opposite reason- because it smelled like a stronger version of whatever was on the other hand (Legend). If I had to choose, I'd choose Percival. Legend is pretty much a skin scent after the first hour on me. That said, at a tenth of the price of Percival, I could carry a decant of Legend in my pocket and just keep respraying whenever I go to the bathroom. I'll probably get it because it's so easy to wear and my wife loves it, but as far as freshies from PDM, I like both Sedley and Greenley better.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/290776">hullhockey91</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2018-10-19">10/19/18 22:16</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Alright guys, here is a 100% honest review. <br />
<br />
I received a sample....I was beyond excited. I threw 4 sprays of the sample on and I was very disappointed. It was something I have smelled before. I couldn't believe it. <br />
<br />
Im pretty sure I had outrageous expectations for PdM. I love Herod, Layton and a few others from them so my expectations were way too high....<br />
<br />
I decided to wear it one last time before I swapped my sample....Well, my mind had made a complete 180 degree turn.<br />
<br />
This stuff was GORGEOUS on my second wearing. I really dove into the scent and found out that it reminded me of Abercrombie &amp; Fitch Fierce as well as Mont Blanc Legend. <br />
<br />
The main difference being...Percival is of outstanding quality. It is top notch. <br />
<br />
Anyone who has ever dreamed of having an expensive smelling Fierce or Legend is now in luck. This stuff is incredible. <br />
<br />
We all know the Fierce and Legend DNA is an absolute crowd pleaser...specifically with the ladies. Well, I can truly say this is going to be even better, strictly because of the quality. It doesn't smell like anything new, but it takes the ever-classic masculine mass-appealing DNA and enhances it into an HD version. <br />
<br />
This is Abercrombie &amp; Fitch Fierce HD. Mont Blanc Legend HD. This is for the more mature burly studs and not the skinny, growing high school dudes. This stuff is powerful, masculine, bad-ass and is going to be a complete compliment monster. <br />
<br />
OVERALL:<br />
<br />
The performance is unbelievable. 4 sprays will last all day and I will get whiffs for 8+ hours. I guess at the end of the day you get what you pay for. <br />
<br />
Scent: 8/10 (Would be a 10, however the DNA has been around)<br />
<br />
Longevity: 9/10 (Insanely good for a fresher frag)<br />
<br />
Projection: 9/10 (Huge scent cloud for the first 2-3 hours and then lingers in air for 8+ hours)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="992970"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=992970#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1654482" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/527536">taskalizer</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-01-17">01/17/20 23:46</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Think Bleu de Chanel too popular? Get this one. Think Dior Sauvage too bland? Get this one. Think Fierce too young and immature? Get this one. Think Platinum Egoiste too barbershop-y and dated? Get this one. Somehow, this is the crossroads where all the above meet and none seems to obey the traffic lights.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="1135536"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=1135536#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="51037" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>
            </div>
</div>
</div><div class="tabs-panel" id="popular-negative-reviews"><div class="cell">
    <div class="strike-title"><span>Most Popular Negative Reviews</span></div>

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1086726" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="DrNDJas"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1063104"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1063104.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="DrNDJas" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Loewe/Loewe-001-Man-EDT-46908.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.46908.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Loewe 001 Man EDT"title="Loewe 001 Man EDT"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1086726ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck6x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1086726" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.71); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1063104">DrNDJas</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-08-11">08/11/19 06:05</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Trigger Warning: this review does NOT reflect snobbery nor the views of a PDM fanboy. Only proceed if you want to read a truthful review. And it ain’t pretty. <br />
You can have the same experience Percival provides for a fraction of the price.  This is a shower gel scent, pure and simple.  If you would like to pay $200 for an olfactory experience most designer houses can provide for under $50, this is your pony!  Perhaps your personal knowledge that you’ve sprayed something “expensive” on your skin gives you an aura of exclusivity. Sure, this kind of thing happens.  But be assured that Percival will not stand out from the designer house herd of modern, synthetic, molecule filled “fresh” scents- for who but an ardent fraghead would even begin to be able to discern a difference? (And I seriously doubt they could either!).  It is not “of higher quality” or “a cut above” it’s designer peers.  No, it just costs more. You’re paying a premium for the right to tell people you’re wearing PDM on this one.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="1086726"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=1086726#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2104167" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; On a daily basis, among regular people, it is the exact same fragrance for a fraction of the price.<br />
<br />
Not worth it for any other purpose than collecting.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="2104167"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=2104167#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1071130" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1071130" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Le Chypriote"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1194785"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1194785.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Le Chypriote" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Giorgio-Armani/Armani-Eau-de-Cedre-31401.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.31401.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Armani Eau de Cèdre"title="Armani Eau de Cèdre"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1071130ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1071130" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1194785">Le Chypriote</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-06-18">06/18/19 13:30</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Does Percival stand out amongst the powerhouses in Parfums De Marly's stable? Yes and no.<br />
<br />
On one hand, it is their most popular freshie, but on the other it doesn't really offer anything unique that would give it the same acclaim as Layton or Carlisle.<br />
<br />
The fragrance itself has a slightly sweet and aromatic freshness, combined with a fruity citrus note and lots of Ambroxan, making it a "loud" and noticeable fragrance. It is a really well blended, high quality "freshie", and will stand out from other crowd pleasers such as Sauvage, Bleu de Chanel, Dylan Blue, and Eros.<br />
<br />
Do not blind buy this one; sample it first.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="1071130"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=1071130#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1097719" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1097719" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="nicolasnmc"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1197863"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="nicolasnmc" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Hermes/Un-Jardin-Sur-Le-Nil-18.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.18.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Un Jardin Sur Le Nil"title="Un Jardin Sur Le Nil"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1097719ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1097719" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1197863">nicolasnmc</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2019-09-14">09/14/19 19:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The worst thing I think a fragrance can be is boring. Unfortunately, I find that to be the case for Percival by Parfums De Marly. The scent definitely features ambroxan and lavender as it’s main notes. There’s not much else that helps this fragrance pop though. It’s very linear and doesn’t change much on skin. I don’t see myself getting many compliments on this. I see many saying it’s a “designer” fragrance but honestly it’s not even that for me... this is unfortunately bland. I can respect fragrances like Bleu De Chanel which despite not smelling unique smells nice and inviting. To me this fragrance unfortunately isn’t anything I’d like to smell like either. It’s an easy wear, yes, but unfortunately there’s just no reason for me to wear this one. If you like the fragrance though it does project decently well and for 5+ hours as moderate projection. Still give it a try if lavender and ambroxan are your thing but unfortunately for me this fragrance didn’t really resonate with me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="1097719"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=1097719#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1225074" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1225074" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="DSC9000"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1249909"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1249909.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="DSC9000" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Chanel/Allure-Homme-Sport-Eau-Extreme-14669.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.14669.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Allure Homme Sport Eau Extreme"title="Allure Homme Sport Eau Extreme"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1225074ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1225074" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1249909">DSC9000</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2020-09-16">09/16/20 08:35</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I can't put my finger on it, but this feels like a scent I've smelled many times before sometime in the '90s. If you were to craft a simple white bottle and label it "Men's Cologne", Percival could be in it. There is something so generic about the DNA. I don't know how this gets labeled unisex. It screams late 20-something who just got his first promotion to management and bought a BMW 3-Series.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="51037"comment_id="1225074"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Parfums-de-Marly/Percival-51037.html?ccid=1225074#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="51037" sentiment="negative"></reviews-infinity>
